id="comp-jp9qnkth" class="KcpHeO tz5f0K comp-jp9qnkth wixui-rich-text" data-testid="richTextElement"><h1 class="font_0 wixui-rich-text__text" style="line-height:normal; font-size:57px;"><span style="letter-spacing:normal;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">Ziqi Lin</span></h1></div></div></div></div></div></section><div id="comp-jpsa5vwh" class="KcpHeO tz5f0K comp-jpsa5vwh wixui-rich-text" data-testid="richTextElement"><h2 class="font_2 wixui-rich-text__text" style="line-height:normal; font-size:19px;"><span style="letter-spacing:normal;" class="wixui-rich-text__text">Bio</span></h2></div><div id="comp-jp9qnkto" class="KcpHeO tz5f0K comp-jp9qnkto wixui-rich-text" data-testid="richTextElement"><p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;">I am a highly motivated individual with a strong passion for data analytics and structural engineering. Currently, I am pursuing my Master of Science in Data Analytics at San Jose State University, California, and I expect to complete my degree in May 2024. Previously, I completed my Master of Science in Structural/Earthquake Engineering from the University of California, Los Angeles in June 2022.</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;"><span class="wixGuard wixui-rich-text__text">​</span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;">I hold a Bachelor of Engineering degree from Southeast University in China, where I pursued an Engineering Intensified Class in Civil Engineering from Chien-Shiung WU College. During my undergraduate studies, I was actively involved in various extracurricular activities, including serving as the Secretary in Charge of Competitions for the Science and Technology Association and as the Commissary in Charge of Psychological&amp;General Affairs for Chien-Shiuang WU College.</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;"><span class="wixGuard wixui-rich-text__text">​</span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;">I have also been recognized for my exceptional skills and abilities, receiving the 17th National College Student Robotics Competition (RoboMaster) National 3rd Prize in July 2018. I have also been granted a patent for my contribution to the development of a Grouting Sleeve Bonding Performance Testing Device, for which I was the first inventor.</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;"><span class="wixGuard wixui-rich-text__text">​</span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;">I possess a diverse range of technical skills, including advanced proficiency in Python, SQL, Tableau, HTML, CAD, and SOLIDWORKS. I also have intermediate-level skills in C++, JavaScript, Swift, Matlab, and R. Additionally, I am fluent in Mandarin and Cantonese and have excellent proficiency in English.</p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;"><span class="wixGuard wixui-rich-text__text">​</span></p>

<p class="font_8 wixui-rich-text__text" style="font-size:15px;">Apart from my academic and technical achievements, I have a wide range of hobbies and interests, including dancing, playing the piano, baking, and skateboarding. I have also volunteered for various organizations, including the Guangzhou Library, LA Pride, and the City of San Jose Animal Care Center.</p></div><div id="comp-jp9qqzm0" class="MazNVa comp-jp9qqzm0
